 *

 *                      {stream} [response] - The HTTP Response stream if an error did not occur.
 */
ServiceFabricClient.prototype.disableNode = function (nodeName, disableNode, options, callback) {
  var client = this;
  if(!callback && typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = null;
  }
  if (!callback) {
    throw new Error('callback cannot be null.');
  }
  // Validate
  try {
    if (nodeName === null || nodeName === undefined || typeof nodeName.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('nodeName cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (disableNode === null || disableNode === undefined) {
      throw new Error('disableNode cannot be null or undefined.');
    }
    if (this.apiVersion === null || this.apiVersion === undefined || typeof this.apiVersion.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('this.apiVersion cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  // Construct URL

                   '//Nodes/{nodeName}/$/Deactivate';
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{nodeName}', encodeURIComponent(nodeName));
  var queryParameters = [];
  queryParameters.push('api-version=' + encodeURIComponent(this.apiVersion));

    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');
  }

  var regex = /([^:]\/)\/+/gi;
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace(regex, '$1');

        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];

  }

  var requestModel = null;
  try {
    if (disableNode !== null && disableNode !== undefined) {
      var requestModelMapper = new client.models['DisableNode']().mapper();
      requestModel = client.serialize(requestModelMapper, disableNode, 'disableNode');
      requestContent = JSON.stringify(requestModel);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    var serializationError = new Error(util.format('Error "%s" occurred in serializing the ' + 
        'payload - "%s"', error.message, util.inspect(disableNode, {depth: null})));

  // Send Request
  return client.pipeline(httpRequest, function (err, response, responseBody) {
    if (err) {
      return callback(err);
    }
    var statusCode = response.statusCode;
    if (statusCode !== 200) {

      error.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
      error.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);

        if (parsedErrorResponse) {
          if (parsedErrorResponse.error) parsedErrorResponse = parsedErrorResponse.error;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.code) error.code = parsedErrorResponse.code;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.message) error.message = parsedErrorResponse.message;

      } catch (defaultError) {
        error.message = util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody ' + 
                         '- "%s" for the default response.', defaultError.message, responseBody);
        return callback(error);
      }
      return callback(error);
    }
    // Create Result
    var result = null;
    if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
    // Deserialize Response
    if (statusCode === 200) {
      var parsedResponse = null;
      try {
        parsedResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        result = JSON.parse(responseBody);

/**

 * health state
 * 
 * @param {string} [options.deployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter] The
 * filter of the deployed service packages health state
 * 
 * @param {object} [options.customHeaders] Headers that will be added to the
 * request
 * 
 * @param {function} callback
 *

ServiceFabricClient.prototype.getDeployedApplicationHealth = function (nodeName, applicationName, options, callback) {
  var client = this;
  if(!callback && typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = null;
  }
  if (!callback) {
    throw new Error('callback cannot be null.');
  }
  var eventsHealthStateFilter = (options && options.eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) ? options.eventsHealthStateFilter : undefined;
  var deployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter = (options && options.deployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter !== undefined) ? options.deployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter : undefined;
  // Validate
  try {
    if (nodeName === null || nodeName === undefined || typeof nodeName.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('nodeName cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (applicationName === null || applicationName === undefined || typeof applicationName.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('applicationName cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (eventsHealthStateFilter !== null && eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined && typeof eventsHealthStateFilter.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('eventsHealthStateFilter must be of type string.');
    }
    if (deployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter !== null && deployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter !== undefined && typeof deployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('deployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter must be of type string.');
    }
    if (this.apiVersion === null || this.apiVersion === undefined || typeof this.apiVersion.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('this.apiVersion cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  // Construct URL
  var requestUrl = this.baseUri +
                   '//Nodes/{nodeName}/$/GetApplications/{applicationName}/$/GetHealth';
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{nodeName}', encodeURIComponent(nodeName));
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{applicationName}', applicationName);
  var queryParameters = [];
  if (eventsHealthStateFilter !== null && eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) {
    queryParameters.push('EventsHealthStateFilter=' + encodeURIComponent(eventsHealthStateFilter));
  }
  if (deployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter !== null && deployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter !== undefined) {
    queryParameters.push('DeployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter=' + encodeURIComponent(deployedServicePackagesHealthStateFilter));
  }
  queryParameters.push('api-version=' + encodeURIComponent(this.apiVersion));
  if (queryParameters.length > 0) {
    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');
  }
  // trim all duplicate forward slashes in the url
  var regex = /([^:]\/)\/+/gi;
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace(regex, '$1');

  // Create HTTP transport objects
  var httpRequest = new WebResource();
  httpRequest.method = 'GET';
  httpRequest.headers = {};
  httpRequest.url = requestUrl;
  // Set Headers

    for(var headerName in options['customHeaders']) {
      if (options['customHeaders'].hasOwnProperty(headerName)) {
        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];
      }

  httpRequest.body = null;
  // Send Request
  return client.pipeline(httpRequest, function (err, response, responseBody) {
    if (err) {
      return callback(err);
    }
    var statusCode = response.statusCode;
    if (statusCode !== 200) {
      var error = new Error(responseBody);
      error.statusCode = response.statusCode;
      error.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
      error.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
      if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
      var parsedErrorResponse;
      try {
        parsedErrorResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedErrorResponse) {
          if (parsedErrorResponse.error) parsedErrorResponse = parsedErrorResponse.error;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.code) error.code = parsedErrorResponse.code;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.message) error.message = parsedErrorResponse.message;
        }
      } catch (defaultError) {
        error.message = util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody ' +

      }
      return callback(error);

    // Deserialize Response
    if (statusCode === 200) {
      var parsedResponse = null;

 *                      {stream} [response] - The HTTP Response stream if an error did not occur.
 */
ServiceFabricClient.prototype.getDeployedServicePackage = function (nodeName, applicationName, options, callback) {
  var client = this;
  if(!callback && typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = null;
  }
  if (!callback) {
    throw new Error('callback cannot be null.');
  }
  // Validate
  try {
    if (nodeName === null || nodeName === undefined || typeof nodeName.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('nodeName cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (applicationName === null || applicationName === undefined || typeof applicationName.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('applicationName cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (this.apiVersion === null || this.apiVersion === undefined || typeof this.apiVersion.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('this.apiVersion cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  // Construct URL
  var requestUrl = this.baseUri +
                   '//Nodes/{nodeName}/$/GetApplications/{applicationName}/$/GetServicePackages';
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{nodeName}', encodeURIComponent(nodeName));
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{applicationName}', applicationName);
  var queryParameters = [];
  queryParameters.push('api-version=' + encodeURIComponent(this.apiVersion));
  if (queryParameters.length > 0) {
    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');
  }
  // trim all duplicate forward slashes in the url
  var regex = /([^:]\/)\/+/gi;
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace(regex, '$1');

  // Create HTTP transport objects
  var httpRequest = new WebResource();
  httpRequest.method = 'GET';
  httpRequest.headers = {};
  httpRequest.url = requestUrl;
  // Set Headers
  if(options) {
    for(var headerName in options['customHeaders']) {
      if (options['customHeaders'].hasOwnProperty(headerName)) {
        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];
      }
    }
  }
  httpRequest.headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json; charset=utf-8';
  httpRequest.body = null;
  // Send Request
  return client.pipeline(httpRequest, function (err, response, responseBody) {
    if (err) {
      return callback(err);
    }
    var statusCode = response.statusCode;
    if (statusCode !== 200) {
      var error = new Error(responseBody);
      error.statusCode = response.statusCode;
      error.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
      error.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
      if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
      var parsedErrorResponse;
      try {
        parsedErrorResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedErrorResponse) {
          if (parsedErrorResponse.error) parsedErrorResponse = parsedErrorResponse.error;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.code) error.code = parsedErrorResponse.code;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.message) error.message = parsedErrorResponse.message;
        }
      } catch (defaultError) {
        error.message = util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody ' + 
                         '- "%s" for the default response.', defaultError.message, responseBody);
        return callback(error);
      }
      return callback(error);
    }
    // Create Result
    var result = null;
    if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
    // Deserialize Response
    if (statusCode === 200) {
      var parsedResponse = null;
      try {

        result = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedResponse !== null && parsedResponse !== undefined) {
          var resultMapper = {
            required: false,
            serializedName: 'parsedResponse',
            type: {
              name: 'Sequence',
              element: {
                  required: false,

                  type: {
                    name: 'Composite',
                    className: 'DeployedServicePackage'
                  }
              }
            }
          };
          result = client.deserialize(resultMapper, parsedResponse, 'result');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        var deserializationError = new Error(util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody - "%s"', error, responseBody));
        deserializationError.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
        deserializationError.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
        return callback(deserializationError);
      }
    }

    return callback(null, result, httpRequest, response);
  });
};

/**

 *

 * 
 * @param {string} [options.eventsHealthStateFilter] The filter of the events
 * health state
 * 
 * @param {object} [options.customHeaders] Headers that will be added to the
 * request
 *

ServiceFabricClient.prototype.getDeployedServicePackageHealth = function (nodeName, applicationName, servicePackageName, options, callback) {
  var client = this;
  if(!callback && typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = null;
  }
  if (!callback) {
    throw new Error('callback cannot be null.');
  }
  var eventsHealthStateFilter = (options && options.eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) ? options.eventsHealthStateFilter : undefined;
  // Validate
  try {
    if (nodeName === null || nodeName === undefined || typeof nodeName.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('nodeName cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (applicationName === null || applicationName === undefined || typeof applicationName.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('applicationName cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (servicePackageName === null || servicePackageName === undefined || typeof servicePackageName.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('servicePackageName cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (eventsHealthStateFilter !== null && eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined && typeof eventsHealthStateFilter.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('eventsHealthStateFilter must be of type string.');
    }
    if (this.apiVersion === null || this.apiVersion === undefined || typeof this.apiVersion.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('this.apiVersion cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  // Construct URL
  var requestUrl = this.baseUri +
                   '//Nodes/{nodeName}/$/GetApplications/{applicationName}/$/GetServicePackages/{servicePackageName}/$/GetHealth';
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{nodeName}', encodeURIComponent(nodeName));
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{applicationName}', applicationName);
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{servicePackageName}', encodeURIComponent(servicePackageName));
  var queryParameters = [];
  if (eventsHealthStateFilter !== null && eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) {
    queryParameters.push('EventsHealthStateFilter=' + encodeURIComponent(eventsHealthStateFilter));
  }
  queryParameters.push('api-version=' + encodeURIComponent(this.apiVersion));
  if (queryParameters.length > 0) {
    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');
  }
  // trim all duplicate forward slashes in the url
  var regex = /([^:]\/)\/+/gi;
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace(regex, '$1');

  // Create HTTP transport objects
  var httpRequest = new WebResource();
  httpRequest.method = 'GET';
  httpRequest.headers = {};
  httpRequest.url = requestUrl;
  // Set Headers
  if(options) {
    for(var headerName in options['customHeaders']) {
      if (options['customHeaders'].hasOwnProperty(headerName)) {
        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];
      }
    }
  }
  httpRequest.headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json; charset=utf-8';
  httpRequest.body = null;
  // Send Request
  return client.pipeline(httpRequest, function (err, response, responseBody) {
    if (err) {
      return callback(err);
    }
    var statusCode = response.statusCode;

      error.statusCode = response.statusCode;
      error.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
      error.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
      if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
      var parsedErrorResponse;
      try {
        parsedErrorResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedErrorResponse) {
          if (parsedErrorResponse.error) parsedErrorResponse = parsedErrorResponse.error;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.code) error.code = parsedErrorResponse.code;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.message) error.message = parsedErrorResponse.message;

      } catch (defaultError) {
        error.message = util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody ' +

        return callback(error);
      }
      return callback(error);
    }
    // Create Result
    var result = null;
    if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
    // Deserialize Response
    if (statusCode === 200) {

  var client = this;

    options = null;

  // Construct URL

    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');

  var regex = /([^:]\/)\/+/gi;

        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];

      error.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);

/**

 *

 * 
 * @param {string} [options.deployedApplicationsHealthStateFilter] The filter
 * of the deployed application health state
 * 
 * @param {object} [options.customHeaders] Headers that will be added to the
 * request
 *

  var client = this;

    callback = options;
    options = null;
  }
  if (!callback) {
    throw new Error('callback cannot be null.');
  }
  var eventsHealthStateFilter = (options && options.eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) ? options.eventsHealthStateFilter : undefined;
  var deployedApplicationsHealthStateFilter = (options && options.deployedApplicationsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) ? options.deployedApplicationsHealthStateFilter : undefined;
  // Validate

    if (applicationName === null || applicationName === undefined || typeof applicationName.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('applicationName cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }

      throw new Error('deployedApplicationsHealthStateFilter must be of type string.');

  }

    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');
  }

  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace(regex, '$1');

    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');

  // trim all duplicate forward slashes in the url
  var regex = /([^:]\/)\/+/gi;
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace(regex, '$1');

  // Create HTTP transport objects
  var httpRequest = new WebResource();
  httpRequest.method = 'GET';
  httpRequest.headers = {};
  httpRequest.url = requestUrl;
  // Set Headers
  if(options) {
    for(var headerName in options['customHeaders']) {
      if (options['customHeaders'].hasOwnProperty(headerName)) {
        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];
      }
    }
  }
  httpRequest.headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json; charset=utf-8';
  httpRequest.body = null;
  // Send Request
  return client.pipeline(httpRequest, function (err, response, responseBody) {
    if (err) {
      return callback(err);
    }
    var statusCode = response.statusCode;
    if (statusCode !== 200) {
      var error = new Error(responseBody);
      error.statusCode = response.statusCode;
      error.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
      error.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
      if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
      var parsedErrorResponse;
      try {
        parsedErrorResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedErrorResponse) {
          if (parsedErrorResponse.error) parsedErrorResponse = parsedErrorResponse.error;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.code) error.code = parsedErrorResponse.code;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.message) error.message = parsedErrorResponse.message;
        }
      } catch (defaultError) {
        error.message = util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody ' + 
                         '- "%s" for the default response.', defaultError.message, responseBody);
        return callback(error);
      }
      return callback(error);
    }
    // Create Result
    var result = null;
    if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
    // Deserialize Response
    if (statusCode === 200) {
      var parsedResponse = null;
      try {
        parsedResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        result = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedResponse !== null && parsedResponse !== undefined) {
          var resultMapper = new client.models['ApplicationUpgrade']().mapper();
          result = client.deserialize(resultMapper, parsedResponse, 'result');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        var deserializationError = new Error(util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody - "%s"', error, responseBody));
        deserializationError.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
        deserializationError.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
        return callback(deserializationError);
      }
    }

    return callback(null, result, httpRequest, response);
  });
};

 * request
 *

 *                      {object} [request]  - The HTTP Request object if an error did not occur.
 *
 *                      {stream} [response] - The HTTP Response stream if an error did not occur.
 */
ServiceFabricClient.prototype.newApplication = function (applicationDescription, options, callback) {
  var client = this;
  if(!callback && typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = null;
  }
  if (!callback) {
    throw new Error('callback cannot be null.');
  }
  // Validate
  try {
    if (applicationDescription === null || applicationDescription === undefined) {
      throw new Error('applicationDescription cannot be null or undefined.');
    }
    if (this.apiVersion === null || this.apiVersion === undefined || typeof this.apiVersion.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('this.apiVersion cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  // Construct URL
  var requestUrl = this.baseUri +
                   '//Applications/$/Create';
  var queryParameters = [];
  queryParameters.push('api-version=' + encodeURIComponent(this.apiVersion));
  if (queryParameters.length > 0) {
    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');
  }

  var regex = /([^:]\/)\/+/gi;
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace(regex, '$1');

  httpRequest.headers = {};
  httpRequest.url = requestUrl;

    for(var headerName in options['customHeaders']) {
      if (options['customHeaders'].hasOwnProperty(headerName)) {
        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];
      }
    }
  }
  httpRequest.headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json; charset=utf-8';
  // Serialize Request
  var requestContent = null;
  var requestModel = null;
  try {
    if (applicationDescription !== null && applicationDescription !== undefined) {
      var requestModelMapper = new client.models['ApplicationDescription']().mapper();
      requestModel = client.serialize(requestModelMapper, applicationDescription, 'applicationDescription');
      requestContent = JSON.stringify(requestModel);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    var serializationError = new Error(util.format('Error "%s" occurred in serializing the ' + 
        'payload - "%s"', error.message, util.inspect(applicationDescription, {depth: null})));
    return callback(serializationError);
  }
  httpRequest.body = requestContent;
  // Send Request
  return client.pipeline(httpRequest, function (err, response, responseBody) {
    if (err) {
      return callback(err);
    }
    var statusCode = response.statusCode;
    if (statusCode !== 200 && statusCode !== 201 && statusCode !== 202) {
      var error = new Error(responseBody);
      error.statusCode = response.statusCode;
      error.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
      error.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
      if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
      var parsedErrorResponse;
      try {
        parsedErrorResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedErrorResponse) {
          if (parsedErrorResponse.error) parsedErrorResponse = parsedErrorResponse.error;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.code) error.code = parsedErrorResponse.code;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.message) error.message = parsedErrorResponse.message;
        }
      } catch (defaultError) {
        error.message = util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody ' + 
                         '- "%s" for the default response.', defaultError.message, responseBody);
        return callback(error);
      }
      return callback(error);
    }
    // Create Result
    var result = null;
    if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
    // Deserialize Response
    if (statusCode === 200) {
      var parsedResponse = null;
      try {
        parsedResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        result = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedResponse !== null && parsedResponse !== undefined) {
          var resultMapper = {
            required: false,
            serializedName: 'parsedResponse',
            type: {
              name: 'String'
            }
          };
          result = client.deserialize(resultMapper, parsedResponse, 'result');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        var deserializationError = new Error(util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody - "%s"', error, responseBody));
        deserializationError.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
        deserializationError.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
        return callback(deserializationError);
      }
    }
    // Deserialize Response
    if (statusCode === 201) {
      var parsedResponse = null;
      try {
        parsedResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        result = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedResponse !== null && parsedResponse !== undefined) {
          var resultMapper = {
            required: false,
            serializedName: 'parsedResponse',
            type: {
              name: 'String'
            }
          };
          result = client.deserialize(resultMapper, parsedResponse, 'result');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        var deserializationError1 = new Error(util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody - "%s"', error, responseBody));
        deserializationError1.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
        deserializationError1.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
        return callback(deserializationError1);
      }
    }
    // Deserialize Response
    if (statusCode === 202) {
      var parsedResponse = null;
      try {
        parsedResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        result = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedResponse !== null && parsedResponse !== undefined) {
          var resultMapper = {
            required: false,
            serializedName: 'parsedResponse',
            type: {
              name: 'String'

    if (applicationName === null || applicationName === undefined || typeof applicationName.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('applicationName cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (this.apiVersion === null || this.apiVersion === undefined || typeof this.apiVersion.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('this.apiVersion cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  // Construct URL
  var requestUrl = this.baseUri +
                   '//Applications/{applicationName}/$/Delete';
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{applicationName}', applicationName);
  var queryParameters = [];
  queryParameters.push('api-version=' + encodeURIComponent(this.apiVersion));
  if (queryParameters.length > 0) {
    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');
  }
  // trim all duplicate forward slashes in the url
  var regex = /([^:]\/)\/+/gi;
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace(regex, '$1');

  // Create HTTP transport objects
  var httpRequest = new WebResource();
  httpRequest.method = 'POST';
  httpRequest.headers = {};
  httpRequest.url = requestUrl;
  // Set Headers
  if(options) {
    for(var headerName in options['customHeaders']) {
      if (options['customHeaders'].hasOwnProperty(headerName)) {
        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];
      }
    }
  }
  httpRequest.headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json; charset=utf-8';
  httpRequest.body = null;
  // Send Request
  return client.pipeline(httpRequest, function (err, response, responseBody) {
    if (err) {
      return callback(err);
    }
    var statusCode = response.statusCode;
    if (statusCode !== 200) {
      var error = new Error(responseBody);
      error.statusCode = response.statusCode;
      error.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
      error.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
      if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
      var parsedErrorResponse;
      try {
        parsedErrorResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedErrorResponse) {
          if (parsedErrorResponse.error) parsedErrorResponse = parsedErrorResponse.error;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.code) error.code = parsedErrorResponse.code;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.message) error.message = parsedErrorResponse.message;
        }
      } catch (defaultError) {
        error.message = util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody ' + 
                         '- "%s" for the default response.', defaultError.message, responseBody);
        return callback(error);
      }
      return callback(error);
    }
    // Create Result
    var result = null;
    if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
    // Deserialize Response
    if (statusCode === 200) {
      var parsedResponse = null;
      try {
        parsedResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        result = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedResponse !== null && parsedResponse !== undefined) {
          var resultMapper = {
            required: false,
            serializedName: 'parsedResponse',
            type: {
              name: 'String'
            }
          };
          result = client.deserialize(resultMapper, parsedResponse, 'result');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        var deserializationError = new Error(util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody - "%s"', error, responseBody));
        deserializationError.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
        deserializationError.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
        return callback(deserializationError);
      }
    }

    return callback(null, result, httpRequest, response);
  });
};

/**
 * @param {string} serviceName The name of the service
 * 
 * @param {object} [options] Optional Parameters.
 * 
 * @param {number} [options.partitionKeyType] The type of the partition key
 * 
 * @param {string} [options.partitionKeyValue] The value of the partition key
 * 
 * @param {string} [options.previousRspVersion] The version of the previous rsp
 * 
 * @param {object} [options.customHeaders] Headers that will be added to the
 * request
 * 
 * @param {function} callback
 *
 * @returns {function} callback(err, result, request, response)
 *
 *                      {Error}  err        - The Error object if an error occurred, null otherwise.
 *
 *                      {object} [result]   - The deserialized result object.
 *                      See {@link ResolvedServicePartition} for more
 *                      information.
 *
 *                      {object} [request]  - The HTTP Request object if an error did not occur.
 *
 *                      {stream} [response] - The HTTP Response stream if an error did not occur.
 */
ServiceFabricClient.prototype.resolveService = function (serviceName, options, callback) {
  var client = this;
  if(!callback && typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = null;
  }
  if (!callback) {
    throw new Error('callback cannot be null.');
  }
  var partitionKeyType = (options && options.partitionKeyType !== undefined) ? options.partitionKeyType : undefined;
  var partitionKeyValue = (options && options.partitionKeyValue !== undefined) ? options.partitionKeyValue : undefined;
  var previousRspVersion = (options && options.previousRspVersion !== undefined) ? options.previousRspVersion : undefined;
  // Validate
  try {
    if (serviceName === null || serviceName === undefined || typeof serviceName.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('serviceName cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (partitionKeyType !== null && partitionKeyType !== undefined && typeof partitionKeyType !== 'number') {
      throw new Error('partitionKeyType must be of type number.');
    }
    if (partitionKeyValue !== null && partitionKeyValue !== undefined && typeof partitionKeyValue.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('partitionKeyValue must be of type string.');
    }
    if (previousRspVersion !== null && previousRspVersion !== undefined && typeof previousRspVersion.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('previousRspVersion must be of type string.');
    }
    if (this.apiVersion === null || this.apiVersion === undefined || typeof this.apiVersion.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('this.apiVersion cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  // Construct URL
  var requestUrl = this.baseUri +
                   '//Services/{serviceName}/$/ResolvePartition';
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{serviceName}', serviceName);
  var queryParameters = [];
  if (partitionKeyType !== null && partitionKeyType !== undefined) {
    queryParameters.push('PartitionKeyType=' + encodeURIComponent(partitionKeyType.toString()));
  }
  if (partitionKeyValue !== null && partitionKeyValue !== undefined) {
    queryParameters.push('PartitionKeyValue=' + encodeURIComponent(partitionKeyValue));
  }
  if (previousRspVersion !== null && previousRspVersion !== undefined) {
    queryParameters.push('PreviousRspVersion=' + encodeURIComponent(previousRspVersion));
  }
  queryParameters.push('api-version=' + encodeURIComponent(this.apiVersion));
  if (queryParameters.length > 0) {
    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');
  }
  // trim all duplicate forward slashes in the url
  var regex = /([^:]\/)\/+/gi;
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace(regex, '$1');

  // Create HTTP transport objects
  var httpRequest = new WebResource();
  httpRequest.method = 'GET';
  httpRequest.headers = {};
  httpRequest.url = requestUrl;
  // Set Headers
  if(options) {
    for(var headerName in options['customHeaders']) {
      if (options['customHeaders'].hasOwnProperty(headerName)) {
        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];
      }
    }
  }
  httpRequest.headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json; charset=utf-8';
  httpRequest.body = null;
  // Send Request
  return client.pipeline(httpRequest, function (err, response, responseBody) {
    if (err) {
      return callback(err);
    }
    var statusCode = response.statusCode;
    if (statusCode !== 200) {
      var error = new Error(responseBody);
      error.statusCode = response.statusCode;
      error.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
      error.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
      if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
      var parsedErrorResponse;
      try {
        parsedErrorResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedErrorResponse) {
          if (parsedErrorResponse.error) parsedErrorResponse = parsedErrorResponse.error;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.code) error.code = parsedErrorResponse.code;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.message) error.message = parsedErrorResponse.message;
        }
      } catch (defaultError) {
        error.message = util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody ' + 
                         '- "%s" for the default response.', defaultError.message, responseBody);
        return callback(error);
      }
      return callback(error);
    }
    // Create Result
    var result = null;
    if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
    // Deserialize Response
    if (statusCode === 200) {
      var parsedResponse = null;
      try {
        parsedResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        result = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedResponse !== null && parsedResponse !== undefined) {

          result = client.deserialize(resultMapper, parsedResponse, 'result');

/**

 * 
 * @param {string} [options.replicasHealthStateFilter] The filter of the
 * replicas health state
 * 
 * @param {object} [options.customHeaders] Headers that will be added to the
 * request
 * 
 * @param {function} callback
 *

ServiceFabricClient.prototype.getPartitionHealth = function (partitionId, options, callback) {
  var client = this;
  if(!callback && typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = null;
  }
  if (!callback) {
    throw new Error('callback cannot be null.');
  }
  var eventsHealthStateFilter = (options && options.eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) ? options.eventsHealthStateFilter : undefined;
  var replicasHealthStateFilter = (options && options.replicasHealthStateFilter !== undefined) ? options.replicasHealthStateFilter : undefined;
  // Validate
  try {
    if (partitionId === null || partitionId === undefined || typeof partitionId.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('partitionId cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (eventsHealthStateFilter !== null && eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined && typeof eventsHealthStateFilter.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('eventsHealthStateFilter must be of type string.');
    }

      throw new Error('replicasHealthStateFilter must be of type string.');
    }

  }

/**
 * @param {string} partitionId The id of the partition
 *

 * 
 * @param {string} [partitionHealthReport.sourceId]
 * 
 * @param {string} [partitionHealthReport.property]
 * 
 * @param {number} [partitionHealthReport.healthState]
 * 
 * @param {string} [partitionHealthReport.description]
 * 
 * @param {string} [partitionHealthReport.timeToLiveInMilliSeconds]
 * 
 * @param {string} [partitionHealthReport.sequenceNumber]
 * 
 * @param {boolean} [partitionHealthReport.removeWhenExpired]
 * 
 * @param {object} [options] Optional Parameters.
 * 
 * @param {object} [options.customHeaders] Headers that will be added to the
 * request
 * 
 * @param {function} callback
 *
 * @returns {function} callback(err, result, request, response)
 *
 *                      {Error}  err        - The Error object if an error occurred, null otherwise.
 *
 *                      {string} [result]   - The deserialized result object.
 *
 *                      {object} [request]  - The HTTP Request object if an error did not occur.
 *
 *                      {stream} [response] - The HTTP Response stream if an error did not occur.
 */
ServiceFabricClient.prototype.sendPartitionHealthReport = function (partitionId, partitionHealthReport, options, callback) {
  var client = this;
  if(!callback && typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = null;
  }
  if (!callback) {
    throw new Error('callback cannot be null.');
  }
  // Validate
  try {
    if (partitionId === null || partitionId === undefined || typeof partitionId.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('partitionId cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
    if (partitionHealthReport === null || partitionHealthReport === undefined) {
      throw new Error('partitionHealthReport cannot be null or undefined.');
    }
    if (this.apiVersion === null || this.apiVersion === undefined || typeof this.apiVersion.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('this.apiVersion cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  // Construct URL
  var requestUrl = this.baseUri +
                   '//Partitions/{partitionId}/$/ReportHealth';
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{partitionId}', encodeURIComponent(partitionId));
  var queryParameters = [];
  queryParameters.push('api-version=' + encodeURIComponent(this.apiVersion));
  if (queryParameters.length > 0) {
    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');
  }
  // trim all duplicate forward slashes in the url
  var regex = /([^:]\/)\/+/gi;
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace(regex, '$1');

  // Create HTTP transport objects
  var httpRequest = new WebResource();
  httpRequest.method = 'POST';
  httpRequest.headers = {};
  httpRequest.url = requestUrl;
  // Set Headers
  if(options) {
    for(var headerName in options['customHeaders']) {
      if (options['customHeaders'].hasOwnProperty(headerName)) {
        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];
      }
    }
  }
  httpRequest.headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json; charset=utf-8';
  // Serialize Request
  var requestContent = null;
  var requestModel = null;
  try {
    if (partitionHealthReport !== null && partitionHealthReport !== undefined) {
      var requestModelMapper = new client.models['PartitionHealthReport']().mapper();
      requestModel = client.serialize(requestModelMapper, partitionHealthReport, 'partitionHealthReport');
      requestContent = JSON.stringify(requestModel);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    var serializationError = new Error(util.format('Error "%s" occurred in serializing the ' + 
        'payload - "%s"', error.message, util.inspect(partitionHealthReport, {depth: null})));
    return callback(serializationError);
  }
  httpRequest.body = requestContent;
  // Send Request
  return client.pipeline(httpRequest, function (err, response, responseBody) {
    if (err) {
      return callback(err);
    }
    var statusCode = response.statusCode;
    if (statusCode !== 200) {
      var error = new Error(responseBody);

/**

ServiceFabricClient.prototype.getReplicaHealth = function (partitionId, replicaId, options, callback) {
  var client = this;
  if(!callback && typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = null;
  }
  if (!callback) {
    throw new Error('callback cannot be null.');
  }
  var eventsHealthStateFilter = (options && options.eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) ? options.eventsHealthStateFilter : undefined;
  // Validate
  try {
    if (partitionId === null || partitionId === undefined || typeof partitionId.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('partitionId cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');

    return callback(error);

  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace('{replicaId}', encodeURIComponent(replicaId));

    queryParameters.push('EventsHealthStateFilter=' + encodeURIComponent(eventsHealthStateFilter));

  }

  httpRequest.method = 'GET';
  httpRequest.headers = {};
  httpRequest.url = requestUrl;
  // Set Headers

      if (options['customHeaders'].hasOwnProperty(headerName)) {
        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];
      }

  }

  httpRequest.body = null;
  // Send Request
  return client.pipeline(httpRequest, function (err, response, responseBody) {
    if (err) {
      return callback(err);
    }

      error.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);

          var resultMapper = new client.models['ClusterLoadInformation']().mapper();
          result = client.deserialize(resultMapper, parsedResponse, 'result');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        var deserializationError = new Error(util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody - "%s"', error, responseBody));
        deserializationError.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
        deserializationError.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
        return callback(deserializationError);
      }
    }

    return callback(null, result, httpRequest, response);
  });
};

/**
 * @param {object} [options] Optional Parameters.
 * 
 * @param {string} [options.eventsHealthStateFilter] The filter of the events
 * health state
 * 
 * @param {string} [options.nodesHealthStateFilter] The filter of the nodes
 * health state
 * 
 * @param {string} [options.applicationsHealthStateFilter] The filter of the
 * applications health state
 * 
 * @param {object} [options.customHeaders] Headers that will be added to the
 * request
 * 
 * @param {function} callback
 *
 * @returns {function} callback(err, result, request, response)
 *
 *                      {Error}  err        - The Error object if an error occurred, null otherwise.
 *
 *                      {object} [result]   - The deserialized result object.
 *                      See {@link ClusterHealth} for more information.
 *
 *                      {object} [request]  - The HTTP Request object if an error did not occur.
 *
 *                      {stream} [response] - The HTTP Response stream if an error did not occur.
 */
ServiceFabricClient.prototype.getClusterHealth = function (options, callback) {
  var client = this;
  if(!callback && typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = null;
  }
  if (!callback) {
    throw new Error('callback cannot be null.');
  }
  var eventsHealthStateFilter = (options && options.eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) ? options.eventsHealthStateFilter : undefined;
  var nodesHealthStateFilter = (options && options.nodesHealthStateFilter !== undefined) ? options.nodesHealthStateFilter : undefined;
  var applicationsHealthStateFilter = (options && options.applicationsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) ? options.applicationsHealthStateFilter : undefined;
  // Validate
  try {
    if (eventsHealthStateFilter !== null && eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined && typeof eventsHealthStateFilter.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('eventsHealthStateFilter must be of type string.');
    }
    if (nodesHealthStateFilter !== null && nodesHealthStateFilter !== undefined && typeof nodesHealthStateFilter.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('nodesHealthStateFilter must be of type string.');
    }
    if (applicationsHealthStateFilter !== null && applicationsHealthStateFilter !== undefined && typeof applicationsHealthStateFilter.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('applicationsHealthStateFilter must be of type string.');
    }
    if (this.apiVersion === null || this.apiVersion === undefined || typeof this.apiVersion.valueOf() !== 'string') {
      throw new Error('this.apiVersion cannot be null or undefined and it must be of type string.');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  // Construct URL
  var requestUrl = this.baseUri +
                   '//$/GetClusterHealth';
  var queryParameters = [];
  if (eventsHealthStateFilter !== null && eventsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) {
    queryParameters.push('EventsHealthStateFilter=' + encodeURIComponent(eventsHealthStateFilter));
  }
  if (nodesHealthStateFilter !== null && nodesHealthStateFilter !== undefined) {
    queryParameters.push('NodesHealthStateFilter=' + encodeURIComponent(nodesHealthStateFilter));
  }
  if (applicationsHealthStateFilter !== null && applicationsHealthStateFilter !== undefined) {
    queryParameters.push('ApplicationsHealthStateFilter=' + encodeURIComponent(applicationsHealthStateFilter));
  }
  queryParameters.push('api-version=' + encodeURIComponent(this.apiVersion));
  if (queryParameters.length > 0) {
    requestUrl += '?' + queryParameters.join('&');
  }
  // trim all duplicate forward slashes in the url
  var regex = /([^:]\/)\/+/gi;
  requestUrl = requestUrl.replace(regex, '$1');

  // Create HTTP transport objects
  var httpRequest = new WebResource();
  httpRequest.method = 'GET';
  httpRequest.headers = {};
  httpRequest.url = requestUrl;
  // Set Headers
  if(options) {
    for(var headerName in options['customHeaders']) {
      if (options['customHeaders'].hasOwnProperty(headerName)) {
        httpRequest.headers[headerName] = options['customHeaders'][headerName];
      }
    }
  }
  httpRequest.headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json; charset=utf-8';
  httpRequest.body = null;
  // Send Request
  return client.pipeline(httpRequest, function (err, response, responseBody) {
    if (err) {
      return callback(err);
    }
    var statusCode = response.statusCode;
    if (statusCode !== 200) {
      var error = new Error(responseBody);
      error.statusCode = response.statusCode;
      error.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
      error.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
      if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
      var parsedErrorResponse;
      try {
        parsedErrorResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedErrorResponse) {
          if (parsedErrorResponse.error) parsedErrorResponse = parsedErrorResponse.error;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.code) error.code = parsedErrorResponse.code;
          if (parsedErrorResponse.message) error.message = parsedErrorResponse.message;
        }
      } catch (defaultError) {
        error.message = util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody ' + 
                         '- "%s" for the default response.', defaultError.message, responseBody);
        return callback(error);
      }
      return callback(error);
    }
    // Create Result
    var result = null;
    if (responseBody === '') responseBody = null;
    // Deserialize Response
    if (statusCode === 200) {
      var parsedResponse = null;
      try {
        parsedResponse = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        result = JSON.parse(responseBody);
        if (parsedResponse !== null && parsedResponse !== undefined) {
          var resultMapper = new client.models['ClusterHealth']().mapper();
          result = client.deserialize(resultMapper, parsedResponse, 'result');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        var deserializationError = new Error(util.format('Error "%s" occurred in deserializing the responseBody - "%s"', error, responseBody));
        deserializationError.request = msRest.stripRequest(httpRequest);
        deserializationError.response = msRest.stripResponse(response);
        return callback(deserializationError);
      }
    }

    return callback(null, result, httpRequest, response);
  });
};
